FIELDWALKING  O  O
2.1  O  O
Introduction  O  O
Fieldwalking  O  O
was  O  O
undertaken  O  O
in  O  O
March  O  O
2005  B-PER  O
,  O  O
as  O  O
the  O  O
first  O  O
part  O  O
of  O  O
the  O  O
evaluation  O  O
.  O  O

It  O  O
is  O  O
a  O  O
survey  O  O
technique  O  O
involving  O  O
the  O  O
systematic  O  O
recovery  O  O
of  O  O
artefacts  O  O
from  O  O
the  O  O
ground  O  O
surface  O  O
.  O  O

The  O  O
distribution  O  O
of  O  O
artefacts  O  O
,  O  O
especially  O  O
the  O  O
identification  O  O
of  O  O
concentrations  O  O
,  O  O
may  O  O
indicate  O  O
the  O  O
location  O  O
of  O  O
past  O  O
human  O  O
activity  O  O
.  O  O

Given  O  O
suitable  O  O
conditions  O  O
(  O  O
including  O  O
soil  O  O
,  O  O
weathering  O  O
,  O  O
crop  O  O
growth  O  O
and  O  O
light  O  O
)  O  O
,  O  O
artefacts  O  O
can  O  O
be  O  O
seen  O  O
within  O  O
ploughed  O  O
soil  O  O
.  O  O

They  O  O
are  O  O
present  O  O
because  O  O
cultivation  O  O
over  O  O
buried  O  O
archaeological  O  O
features/deposits  O  O
results  O  O
in  O  O
the  O  O
movement  O  O
of  O  O
artefacts  O  O
into  O  O
the  O  O
overlying  O  O
plough  O  O
soil  O  O
.  O  O

The  O  O
purpose  O  O
of  O  O
the  O  O
fieldwalking  O  O
was  O  O
to  O  O
systematically  O  O
collect  O  O
artefacts  O  O
from  O  O
the  O  O
surface  O  O
of  O  O
the  O  O
development  O  O
area  O  O
.  O  O

The  O  O

GEOPHYSICAL  O  O
SURVEY  O  O
3.1  O  O
Introduction  O  O
Changes  O  O
in  O  O
magnetic  O  O
responses  O  O
below  O  O
the  O  O
ploughsoil  O  O
can  O  O
indicate  O  O
variations  O  O
in  O  O
the  O  O
subsoil/geology  O  O
some  O  O
of  O  O
which  O  O
may  O  O
be  O  O
associated  O  O
with  O  O
buried  O  O
archaeological  O  O
features  O  O
.  O  O

The  O  O
means  O  O
by  O  O
which  O  O
these  O  O
variations  O  O
are  O  O
identified  O  O
and  O  O
located  O  O
is  O  O
known  O  O
as  O  O
a  O  O
geophysical  O  O
survey  O  O
.  O  O

Geophysical  O  O
surveys  O  O
are  O  O
particularly  O  O
effective  O  O
in  O  O
locating  O  O
ditch  B-CON  O
es  I-CON  O
and  O  O
large  B-CON  O
pits  I-CON  O
,  O  O
but  O  O
can  O  O
not  O  O
always  O  O
locate  O  O
smaller  O  O
features  O  O
such  O  O
as  O  O
postholes  B-CON  O
and  O  O
small  B-CON  O
pits  I-CON  O
.  O  O

This  O  O
means  O  O
that  O  O
the  O  O
absence  O  O
of  O  O
evidence  O  O
provided  O  O
by  O  O
a  O  O
geophysical  O  O
survey  O  O
can  O  O
not  O  O
be  O  O
taken  O  O
as  O  O
a  O  O
categorical  O  O
indication  O  O
of  O  O
the  O  O
absence  O  O
of  O  O
archaeological  O  O
features  O  O
.  O  O

field  O  O
with  O  O

approximately  O  O

on  O  O
a  O  O
base  O  O

.  O  O

The  O  O

.  O  O

relatively  O  O

also  O  O
means  O  O
that  O  O

.  O  O

'  O  O

not  O  O

assumed  O  O
to  O  O

of  O  O
any  O  O
